Employees of Various Industries Report Smuggling Jointly - Telegram to the Whole Country for Consistent Reporting - This City Started Working Yesterday - Eight Reporting Measures Set

The Joint Smuggling Reporting Committee of Employees of Various Industries has been actively proceeding with the smuggling reporting work since its establishment, and has set eight reporting measures, and telegrammed them to employees of various industries across the country for consistent implementation. Here is a detailed report by the Dagong Society reporter:

Start Reporting

The Smuggling Reporting Committee of Employees of Various Industries in this city has decided to start smuggling reporting work from yesterday after its establishment. All employees of various industries in this city can contact the committee for reporting smuggled goods. The office is temporarily located at No. 545, Erma Road, Shanghai Workers' Society, and the first committee meeting will be held on the 13th of this month to discuss various important matters. Employees from various places are also enthusiastically reporting to the committee to participate.

Reporting Measures The committee will assist the government in reporting smuggling. If smuggled goods are found, no matter how much, they should be reported immediately. After discovering smuggled goods, employees should report them to the committee in writing or verbally. However, the reporter must provide their name and address, but the committee will absolutely keep their identity secret. If the reported smuggled goods do not match the facts, the committee will impose sanctions. The reporter should fill in the detailed information of the merchant factory and the person in charge of transporting the smuggled goods. After receiving the report, the committee will send staff to secretly investigate and report it to the competent authority for handling. If the smuggled goods were not detected when they were transported in, or until they were disguised and impersonated as domestic goods or other foreign goods for sale, the trademark that was replaced, the smuggled goods, and the standards for distinguishing them from other goods should be sent to the committee together. The committee will send staff to investigate, or ask experts to inspect, and then report it to the competent authority for handling. The committee will give nominal rewards to employees who report smuggling to encourage patriots. If there are special merits in reporting, it will be reported to the competent authority for material rewards. If employees who report smuggling are suspended or otherwise harmed by the store or factory, the committee will resolutely protect them and petition the competent authority to protect them, so that the reporting employees will not suffer any spiritual or material losses. If the staff sent by the committee to investigate smuggling collude with the other party who is transporting smuggled goods, cover up the truth, or take bribes to let them go, or fabricate reports, they will be paraded through the streets or reported to the competent authority to be held liable for instigating the crime and the crime of accomplice. These measures will be implemented from the date of promulgation.

Telegram to the Whole Country

The Shanghai Municipal Employees Smuggling Reporting Committee telegraphed the whole country, saying: (Title omitted) Since Japanese and Korean vagrants smuggled goods in North China, the loss of customs revenue has reached more than 100 million yuan. The damage to the country's vitality and the shaking of the national economy are becoming increasingly serious. Our people are in this bad environment, and we are truly heartbroken. A group of traitors who have lost their conscience and act as accomplices, taking advantage of the protection of foreign slaves, and being blinded by profits, are transporting a large number of smuggled goods, which are really the moths of the country and the enemies of the nation. Our employees are members of the nation. Loving the country and the nation is our bounden duty. We cannot remain silent and allow them to be rampant. The employees of various industries in Shanghai have established the Smuggling Reporting Committee on this day and will announce the reporting measures on Geng day to start the reporting work. Our employees should stand on the front line of saving the nation and eradicating evil, not seeking merit, but wishing to have no fault. This heart and this purpose shine like the sky. I urge my employees across the country to take the same steps, implement them immediately, assist the government, and eliminate the scourge. We will fight a death match against treacherous merchants who transport smuggled goods. This is a small wish, and I hope you will understand.

Yesterday's Establishment: Fish Industry Smuggling Inspection Committee Issues Declaration Urging Attention from All Sectors

Smuggling in North China is becoming increasingly serious, and various smuggled goods are spreading throughout Shanghai. Although the government has strictly formulated anti-smuggling measures and implemented them vigorously, a general group of unscrupulous people still drink poison to quench their thirst and have no scruples. Jin Chuxiang, in view of this situation, in order to strengthen the organization of the fish industry and assist the government in intensifying anti-smuggling efforts, specially joined forces with key figures in the industry to form the Shanghai Fish Industry Smuggling Inspection Committee, which began inspection work yesterday. At the same time, a declaration was issued to urge attention from all sectors. The declaration stated, "Japan, under the pretext of the Boxer Protocol and the Tanggu Truce, has increased its troops in North China and sheltered smuggling. Although our government has repeatedly negotiated, it has been ineffective due to Japan's tough attitude. Recently, the smuggling trend has spread throughout the country. If it is not quickly eradicated, the impact will not only cause endless losses to the national treasury, but also the weak domestic industry and commerce will be completely destroyed. The national economy will inevitably collapse. Looking at the future, we cannot help but shudder. Now the government has promulgated measures to prevent smuggling by road transport, interim regulations for punishing tax evasion, and interim regulations for inspecting the import and sale of goods, and has issued orders to various places to strictly implement them. If local industries and businesses can all uphold their patriotic sincerity and deeply feel the pain, and agree to refrain from purchasing and selling smuggled goods, then by supporting each other from top to bottom, smuggling will naturally be eradicated. However, people's hearts are not as they used to be, and unscrupulous merchants are emerging one after another. Chuxiang and others, speaking about fish in terms of fish, based on past experience in cracking down on unscrupulous merchants colluding with foreigners to encroach on fishing rights, believe that in order to thoroughly eliminate smuggled goods, it is essential for enthusiastic patriots or legitimate merchants in various industries to form strict organizations and conduct their own inspections. Therefore, based on this principle, the Fish Industry Smuggling Inspection Committee was organized, and work began immediately. From now on, regardless of whether they are in the same industry or not, if any smuggling of fish products is discovered, they will be reported according to the law and severely punished. We hope that all sectors will be aware of this. This declaration is hereby issued."

Ministry of Communications Sends Personnel to Investigate; Jardine Matheson Disrupts Shipping Rights; National and Private Shipping Companies Resist on Reasonable Grounds; Gansu Ship to Sail to Lianyungang for Its Maiden Voyage

Since the British company Jardine Matheson & Co. suspended operations of its original ships due to sluggish business on the Northern Lines and switched to the Lianyungang Line of the Longhai Railway, the Gansu ship has already made its maiden voyage on the 7th. National and private shipping companies in Shanghai have resisted on reasonable grounds. After the Ministry of Communications sent personnel to Shanghai to investigate, it immediately consulted the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to protest to the company. The following is an account of the situation obtained by a reporter from the Ta Kung Pao:

Jardine Matheson's Gansu to Begin Regular Sailing

The Chengdu, Zhejiang, Gansu, Chongqing, and other ships of the British Jardine Matheson & Co., which operate on the Northern Lines, have suspended service at the beginning of this month due to the large number of commercial ships operating on the lines and sluggish business. They will switch to the Lianyungang Line of the Longhai Railway. The Gansu ship, with a load of 2,000 tons, is scheduled to load passengers and cargo in Shanghai on the 15th of this month and officially set sail for the port. By the end of this month, all the Chengdu, Zhejiang, and Chongqing ships will also be added to the line.

National and Private Companies Resist on Reasonable Grounds

Since learning that Jardine Matheson & Co. is opening the Lianyungang shipping line, national-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and privately-run Da Zhen, Hezhong and other shipping companies in Shanghai not only believe it will affect their business, but also disrupt China's shipping rights. They have telegraphed the Ministry of Communications to protest on reasonable grounds. The private sector has also petitioned the Shanghai Shipping Guild to submit a request to the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau, which will then forward it to the Ministry of Communications for serious negotiations in order to safeguard shipping merchants and protect sovereignty. The guild also plans to convene a meeting within days to discuss effective countermeasures.

Ministry of Communications Sends Personnel to Shanghai to Investigate

Yesterday, inquiries were made to the local transportation authorities. After receiving telegrams from various parties requesting to stop the British Jardine Matheson & Co. from opening the Lianyungang shipping line, the Ministry of Communications, in order to clarify the facts and strive for a solution, will send personnel to Shanghai within days to conduct an investigation. After the investigation, it will decide to consult the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to lodge a serious protest with the British Embassy in order to achieve the goal of safeguarding China's maritime administrative sovereignty.

Ministry of Foreign Affairs Replies to Chamber of Commerce Regarding Protests Against Increased Troops and Smuggling

Exchange Rate Between Shanghai and Guangdong Gradually Rebounds; Yesterday It Was 666 Yuan per 1,000 Yuan; Foreign Exchange Stable, Equilibrium Tax Up 5 Percent

The exchange rate between Shanghai and Guangdong has gradually rebounded after official and commercial banks and the Guangdong Provincial Department of Finance made every effort to maintain the credit of Guangdong banknotes and stipulated four measures to stabilize finance, including prohibiting short selling and military personnel from purchasing Hong Kong dollars. Yesterday, the Shanghai-Guangdong exchange rate was 666 yuan in legal currency per 1,000 Guangdong silver dollars, an increase of six yuan compared to 660 yuan per 1,000 yuan last Saturday. It is expected to continue to rise, and it will not be difficult to restore the original state in the short term. The foreign exchange prices quoted by the Central Bank yesterday still adhered to the standard price principle and remained stable as before. The prices are recorded as follows: London, one national currency unit, equivalent to one shilling and two and a half pence; New York, 30 US dollars; Paris, 460.5 francs; Berlin, 75.25 marks; Japan, 103 yen; Hong Kong, 94 Hong Kong dollars (the above are all prices converted per 100 yuan). The price of silver has risen slightly compared to before, with large bars of silver at 20 pence. The equilibrium tax has also risen to 5%. The standard price of Shanghai standard gold is 1,128.3 yuan, the interest spread is 8%, and the consumption tax on customs duties is 2.241 yuan per legal currency yuan.

Shanghai Citizens' Year for National Products; Planning to Expand Propaganda Week; Board Meeting to Be Held Tomorrow to Discuss Implementation

The Shanghai Citizens' Year for National Products National Products Movement Committee, in view of the increasingly rampant smuggling in North China and the severe damage to national products, in order to arouse the public to consume domestic products and eliminate smuggled goods, is preparing for the Second National Products Movement Propaganda Conference and has scheduled a meeting of the entire board of directors for 4:00 PM tomorrow (the 10th) to discuss implementation measures. Details are recorded below:

Board Meeting to Be Held Tomorrow

Since the Citizens' Year for National Products was established on New Year's Day this year, it has been actively promoting domestic products. In view of the smuggling in North China, a meeting of the entire board of directors will be held tomorrow afternoon. A special notice was sent to all directors yesterday: "Dear Directors, recently, smuggling in North China has become increasingly serious, and national products have been severely damaged, which will lead to bankruptcy. In order to discuss the prevention of smuggling and promote domestic products, it is hereby scheduled to hold a meeting of the entire board of directors at 4:00 PM on the 10th of this month (Wednesday) on the third floor of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce at Tianhou Palace Bridge to discuss implementation measures. A special notice is hereby issued. We hope that you will attend at that time to discuss the progress together."

Preparing for Total Mobilization Propaganda Week

In order to widely promote domestic products and achieve practical results, the association is preparing for a Total Mobilization Propaganda Week for National Products, scheduled to begin on the 20th of this month. The propaganda schedule has been set. The first day (June 20th) is Citizens' Propaganda Day, led by the citizens' federations of the first and second special districts. The district branches are also requested to lead the citizens in each district under the leadership of the Kuomintang district headquarters to form propaganda teams and set out to promote. A propaganda conference will be held at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce on the afternoon of the same day, and all participating citizens will take an oath to consume domestic products. The second day (the 21st) is National Products Factory Propaganda Day, led by national product organizations throughout the city, to hold national product sample trademark exhibitions in various national product factories. The fifth day (the 24th) is Entertainment Propaganda Day. The National Products Year Committee will submit a request to the Kuomintang and government agencies, informing all industrial, commercial, and academic organizations to prepare lanterns and participate in the parade, and send a letter to various national product organizations to lead manufacturers to participate. Cotton Control Council and Banking Sector to Visit Salt Reclamation Area in Northern Jiangsu; Preparing for Improvement of Cotton Industry and Investment; Delegation of More Than Ten People to Depart on the Evening of the 10th

The National Economic Council's Cotton Control Council and the banking sector, at the invitation of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, will visit the cotton planting areas in the salt reclamation area in northern Jiangsu to prepare for the improvement of the cotton industry and investment. The Cotton Control Council and various banks have appointed experts and are scheduled to depart by ship on the 10th. Details are recorded below:

Scheduled Departure

Those invited to visit this time, in addition to the Cotton Control Council, include more than ten banks, including the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, Zhongnan Bank, Yanye Bank, Jincheng Bank, Dalu Bank, Xingye Bank, China Farmers Bank, and Jiangsu Farmers Bank. The Cotton Control Council has appointed cotton planting experts Li Shengbo, Bian Bingwen, and Tong Runfu and others, a total of four people, to accompany more than ten people from various banks. They are scheduled to depart from Shanghai on the Daqing ship of the Dada Company on the evening of the 10th and go directly to Nantong.

Visiting Area

On the 12th, they will arrive in Nantong and be accompanied by staff from the Jiangsu Provincial Government to visit cotton planting areas in the salt reclamation areas in Nantong, Rugao, Haian, Dongtai, and Xinfengji. Then, they will go to Chenjiagang and Baojiadun in Haizhou. The itinerary is scheduled for half a month, and they will return to Shanghai around the 20th of this month. The purpose of this visit is to focus on investment. Because cotton production in northern Jiangsu has increased in recent years, and with the completion of the new canal, agriculture in the area will have a rapid development trend. In the future, it can be the best area for the banking sector to invest in rural areas.

Overview of Reclamation Area

The salt reclamation area in northern Jiangsu is extremely vast, stretching from Lvsizhen in Nantong to Chenjiagang in Haizhou, with an area of about 600 li from north to south and east to west. It was originally a swamp used for storing grass and boiling salt. Although there were already 3.8 million mu of reclaimed land, about 10 million mu of wasteland remained, and all of it was fertile land, which was very suitable for planting cotton. Therefore, once all the wasteland is reclaimed, it will be the largest source of wealth in Jiangsu Province.

Taxpaying Chinese Association of the French Concession Requests Improvement of Concession's Tax Collection Methods; Improper Classification of Business Tax; Review Fees Not Assessed According to Standards

Tax collection methods of the French Concession Public Works Department Tax Bureau, including improper classification of business tax, review fees not assessed according to standards, and unreasonable fines imposed by the Sanitation Department without allowing citizens to appeal, have been a concern of taxpaying Chinese in the Concession. They have written to the Taxpaying Chinese Association of the French Concession requesting negotiations regarding the improper classification of business and sanitation tax, the uncertain assessment of review fees, the prompt implementation of reduced housing tax, and the arbitrary penalties imposed by the Sanitation Department. The Taxpayers Association sent a letter to the French Concession Public Works Department yesterday, ordering the responsible personnel to improve the situation. The original text is recorded as follows:

Improper Classification of Business Tax

"Dear Sir, according to the taxpaying Chinese in the Concession, there have been many complaints about the improper classification of business and sanitation tax, the uncertain assessment of review fees, the prompt implementation of reduced housing tax, and the arbitrary penalties imposed by the Sanitation Department. We hereby request negotiations. The revised business and sanitation tax regulations were promulgated in 1936 and divided into four levels: A, B, C, and D. There are no clear regulations regarding the classification standards. In addition, the original maximum amount for review fees was ten yuan, but as stated in Article 6, Item 4 of the regulations, the review fee for small businesses in categories A, B, C, and D opened in Chinese-style single-room houses may be reduced to two yuan. Also, according to the same item, the review fee for small industries in the second table of category B businesses may be reduced to one yuan. However, inspectors rarely assess according to the standards. The tax grade is entirely based on the speculation and conjecture of the inspectors, which has become the focus of recent disputes between the bureau and the citizens. For example:

Focus of Disputes Over Increased Taxes

(A) Regarding the increased tax portion: Yingkang Medical Garden at No. 150-152 Rue du Père Huc, which was originally 2.8 yuan, has now increased to 7 yuan. Fuzhengyuan Wine Store at No. 12 Rue du Père Huc, which was originally 1.4 yuan, has now increased to 2.8 yuan. Xiqingyong Wine Store at No. 64 Rue Gandi, which was originally 1.4 yuan, has now increased to 2.8 yuan. Zhang Hongsheng Wine Store at No. 180 Avenue Blanchy, which was originally 1.4 yuan, has now increased to 2.8 yuan. There is no clear notification of the standards and basis for these tax increases. If the size of the storefront is the standard, then the storefronts of the four stores remain the same and have not been expanded. If the prosperity of the business is the standard, then the businesses of the four stores have not improved and are not as prosperous as before. Since there are no standards to follow, these tax increases are unacceptable to the stores and are truly unreasonable.

Review Fees Should Be Fair

(B) Regarding the review fees: 1. Yu Feng Company at No. 101 Ningbo Road only rents one room. The width and size, as well as the number of employees, all meet the requirements for a small business, but the Tax Bureau forced them to pay a review fee of ten yuan. The improper collection of review fees is a widespread situation, and Yu Feng Company is not the only one. According to the regulations, the maximum amount is ten yuan. If the residence and the furnishings of the store belong to a small business, then the fee may be reduced to two yuan or one yuan. There are many differences between two yuan, one yuan, and ten yuan. A careful interpretation of the meaning of the provisions requires the inspector to examine the size of the business and then assess the fee. If it is not necessary to pay ten yuan, then how much should be paid? The most fair perspective should be used to estimate. However, inspectors often do not examine carefully and simply say two yuan or ten yuan. Other amounts are never heard of. As a result, merchants are wronged by arbitrary decisions beyond counting. Yu Feng Company is just one example, and there are many others. This is what we hope the Tax Bureau will rectify.

Request for Housing Tax Reduction According to Proportions

Furthermore, in the 1936 budget of the Public Works Department, it was stated that when the rent is used as the basis for the rental value, the total amount of rent should be reduced proportionally according to the amount of benefits enjoyed by the tenant from the landlord for calculation purposes. 1. If the rent includes tap water supply, it should be reduced by 5%. 2. For houses with electricity supply, the rent should be reduced by 5%. 3. For rent that includes garbage incineration facilities, it should be reduced by 10%. 4. For houses with electrical equipment, the rent should be reduced by 10%. Although the regulations have been promulgated, the reductions have not yet been implemented, which has led to questions from taxpayers. The Public Works Department should order the rent collection agencies in the Concession to promptly report the rent situation for verification and reduction in order to be practical.

Arbitrary Penalties by the Sanitation Department Should Be Improved

Furthermore, there is a great need to improve the methods for unsanitary penalty cases in the Concession. Currently, Public Works Department investigators only target places where garbage is piled up. As a result, false penalties are heard of every day, and when people are falsely accused, the police do not allow them to appeal and even beat them, which is very improper. In another case, Ruixing Restaurant at No. 153 Route Conty was punished by the Public Works Department for unsanitary conditions because it was ordered by the West Patrol to clean up the garbage left by street vendors. This kind of measure is particularly absurd and should be ordered to be corrected by the Tax Bureau to avoid unjustly accusing the innocent. All of the above situations are widespread in the Concession and are the most disputed situations. We hope that you will order the responsible personnel to improve them quickly and look forward to your reply. Respectfully, to the General Manager of the French Concession Public Works Department, Mr. Badet."

The National Physicians Association Calls for the Protection of Medical Rights; Medical Talents Should Be Respected by Society; the Current Physician Regulations are Insufficient to Guarantee Protection

The Shanghai National Physicians Association yesterday submitted a document to the Ministry of Health, stating that the Physician Law and the Physician Guild Law have not yet been promulgated, and medical rights have lost their protection.

It earnestly requests that measures be taken to provide relief. Medicine is the culmination of scientific achievements, and progress has only been achieved today through gradual academic programs, considerable time, and rigorous study and practice. Therefore, medical talents should be respected by society. In advanced countries, medical rights are guaranteed by national laws. Not only are there clear provisions in the Physician Law, but also the Physician Guild Law, which allows for the combined efforts of the same profession to supervise, encourage, and safeguard rights and interests, thereby supplementing the inadequacies of the law. This is also an expression of valuing medical talents. Old Chinese medicine is crude and absurd, and has long been despised by the literati. Only those who have failed in both learning and swordsmanship retreat to study medicine. After reading a little of the Tangtou Song Formula, they go out to practice medicine. Since their learning is so superficial, society regards them as lowly witches, and it is appropriate that they do not have the protection of national laws. In the past thirty years, thanks to the government's advocacy and promotion of new medicine, efforts have not been spared, and talents have gradually increased and practical results have become increasingly apparent. However, society's ingrained negative attitude towards medicine has not changed slightly. Even administrative officials cannot avoid being misled by popular views, and there are even those who undermine medical rights. At the fourth national congress convened by the association, members from various regions reported that they were suffering from the arbitrary and harsh regulations and exorbitant taxes imposed by provincial and county authorities, or from the arbitrary exercise of power and abuse of authority by public security personnel. The losses in business and spirit were difficult to describe in detail. Therefore, there was a proposal to request the Ministry to set up a method for relief. After discussion by the conference, it was generally believed that this phenomenon was inevitable before the promulgation of the Physician Law and the Physician Guild Law. The current Provisional Physician Regulations can be used as a basis, but the content is too sketchy and insufficient to protect medical rights. Therefore, it was resolved to earnestly request that all levels of主管官吏官吏 be notified to invite local physicians' guilds to send representatives to attend and contribute opinions to the formulation of local single medical and health regulations before the promulgation of such regulations, so that there would be no bias and it would be easy to implement. It is also hoped that the public security authorities will be strictly ordered to be cautious about abusing their authority and that formal physicians should not be arrested, detained, or interrogated and punished in order to respect medicine and safeguard medical rights. In addition, Article 4 of the current Provisional Physician Regulations, which does not grant physician certificates, Clause 1, those who have been sentenced to more than three years of imprisonment for reasons other than engaging in the National Revolution, since the implementation of the new criminal law, this provision has been overly harsh. Article 276, Section 2 of the New Criminal Law states that those engaged in business who commit the crime in the preceding paragraph (negligent homicide) due to negligence in their business shall be sentenced to imprisonment of not more than five years. If a doctor is accidentally invoked by this article due to an unavoidable accident and sentenced to three years of imprisonment, according to the provisions of the preceding Provisional Physician Regulations, he will never be able to practice medicine again. Not only is there a sense of light crime and heavy punishment for doctors, but also for the sake of national talent, the loss is also great and superficial. Therefore, the conference also resolved to earnestly request the government to submit a request to the court for amendment. All of these aspects are closely related to the interests of the new medical community.

Therefore, based on the resolutions, a document is submitted to the senior officials, who are requested to consider that the Physician Law and the Physician Guild Law have not yet been promulgated and that medical rights have no protection at all, and to generously provide appropriate maintenance, adopt my humble opinions, and implement them promptly, so as to reduce the losses of our new medical community in terms of work and spirit. This is truly convenient for the public. Respectfully submitted to the Director of the Ministry of Health, Liu,

Issuing Six-Percent Bonds to Complete the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway; Totaling £1.1 Million with a Term of 25 Years; Underwritten by the Sino-British Chinese Construction Bank Corporation

In order to complete the Zhapu to Cao'e River section of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway and the Hangzhou-Shaoxing section, and to jointly build the Qiantang River Bridge with the Zhejiang Provincial Government, the Ministry of Railways obtained a loan of 16 million yuan from the Chinese Construction Bank Corporation and the Sino-British Bank Corporation in October 1934, with an interest rate of 5.5 percent. The Ministry of Railways has now agreed with the two banks to revise the loan contract to be 1.1 million pounds, equivalent to more than 18 million yuan in national currency, with the annual interest rate changed to 6 percent. Sterling six-percent bonds will be issued and underwritten by the two banks. The contract has now been approved by the Legislative Yuan, and the syndicate is allowed to issue bonds soon. According to a report by a reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency, the face value of the bonds will be denominated in sterling, divided into three types: £10, £50, and £100. They will not be circulated on the market in the future, but will be underwritten by the two banks and sold abroad. The credit of Chinese railway bonds in the foreign market is well-known, and foreigners are happy to buy them. The term is 25 years, starting from July 1941, and the principal will be repaid twice a year until it is fully repaid in 1961. The Ministry of Railways will establish a fund management committee to oversee the repayment of principal and interest.

After the Chinese Yangtze River Pilots Petition, the Central Government Agrees to be Managed by the Ministry of Communications; the Ministry of Civil Training Has Drafted Measures; It is Decided to Request the Government to Promulgate a Pilotage Law

Chinese Yangtze River pilotage representatives Feng Fucheng and others, who went to Beijing to petition, returned to Shanghai the night before last, having achieved satisfactory results in Beijing, and released the following details of the petition to visitors:

Purpose of the Request

The purpose of the Chinese Yangtze River pilots' petition is to promulgate a pilotage law to reclaim pilotage rights and abolish the Shanghai Pilotage Management Committee, transferring full management to the Ministry of Communications. Previously, China did not pay attention to pilotage rights, resulting in them being controlled by foreigners. After the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, it gradually began to pay attention to this, and in 1929, the Naval Ministry established a pilotage training institute, training more than 300 qualified students. In 1933, the Ministries of Finance, Navy, Communications, and Staff jointly formed the Shanghai Pilotage Management Committee, which was originally established to protect Chinese nationals. However, the customs commissioner representing the Ministry of Finance still held the position of chairman, and representatives of foreign chambers of commerce participated. Not only did they disregard the legal qualifications of the Naval Ministry's pilotage training institute, but they also implemented control over Chinese pilots on the Yangtze River, while providing convenience for foreign personnel, allowing them to develop and not restricting them. The government's reclamation was a mere formality, the suffering of the Chinese people and the danger to national defense were even greater than before. Therefore, Chinese Yangtze River pilots believe this is a major concern and have repeatedly called for help and requested assistance from all sectors of the country to achieve the goal of complete reclamation as soon as possible in order to strengthen sovereignty and maintain national defense.

Petition Process

The representatives arrived in Beijing on the 3rd of this month and submitted petitions to the Central Ministry of Civil Training and the Executive Yuan. The opinions they raised were accepted by the authorities, and the results were very satisfactory. The Ministry of Civil Training has also drafted measures and expressed to the representatives that it is determined to request the government to promulgate a pilotage law to reclaim pilotage rights, abolish the pilotage management committee, and transfer the pilotage personnel to the full management of the Ministry of Communications. Therefore, the representatives considered themselves satisfied and returned to Shanghai yesterday. According to Mr. Feng, the petition in Beijing was supported by all sectors and the maritime organizations, for which they are deeply grateful.

The Preparatory Committee of the Special District Meat Industry Held an Emergency Meeting Yesterday to Discuss the Organization of an Investigation Team to Rectify Market Prices; Requesting the Municipal Council to Prohibit the Use of Balance Scales

The fresh meat industry in this city has recently faced difficulties in its operation due to the scarcity of pig sources and soaring pig prices. On the 6th of last month, the Shanghai Meat Industry Guild collectively discussed price increases. It is learned that the industry in the special district still does not sell according to the stipulated prices. At the same time, it is affected by other industry members and citizens not using market scales. Therefore, they have filed requests with the Preparatory Committee of the First Special District Branch of the Shanghai Fresh Meat Industry Guild, requesting immediate and strict rectification. After receiving the report, the committee convened an emergency meeting of the preparatory committee yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM. More than 20 people attended, including Wu Gensheng, Fan Deyi, Rong Fuchang, and Chen Longhu. The meeting was chaired by Sun Hongyang and recorded by Mao Yicheng. The chairman first reported the significance of the meeting. Then, the following cases were immediately resolved: (A) In recent days, more industry members have come to the association claiming that the prices stipulated by the representatives' meeting on the 6th of last month (which were publicly announced by the Shanghai Fresh Meat Industry Guild in the newspaper) have not been followed by a small number of industry members to this day. At the same time, restaurants, noodle shops, kitchens, and citizens are not using market scales, making it difficult to operate. It is necessary to strictly rectify this. As a result, no clues were obtained, and it should be decided what to do. It was resolved that the association should send a letter to the general guild, requesting that the Social Bureau forward it to the Municipal Council to notify all industries to use market scales uniformly, and to send patrols to prohibit citizens from carrying balance scales to ensure fairness. An investigation team should be organized by the association to go to various districts to investigate. If there are those who still do not sell according to the stipulated prices, they should be strictly advised; otherwise, the pig market should be notified to stop their dealings. At the same time, industry members must not collude; otherwise, the industry member will be subject to the same regulations. The investigators will be issued badges and printed photos by the association for identification. If the investigators have not found out, but the industry members know about it, they should immediately report it to the association. After the investigation is confirmed, the measures resolved in the second item will be implemented. (B) The case of recommending investigators for various districts was resolved to recommend 30 people, including Wu Gensheng, as investigators. (C) The case of reporting the above resolutions to all industry members immediately was resolved to send notices to inform all industry members. The meeting adjourned after the resolutions were made.

The Weather Resembles Late Autumn; Wind and Rain Again in This Port; This Year's Rainfall Exceeds Last Year's; Abnormal Weather Rarely Seen in Recent Years

Local Weather: This year has been particularly marked by much rain and little sunshine. Since the beginning of summer, the weather has been consistently cool and cold, unlike summer. The night before last, there was wind and rain throughout the night, which continued until yesterday morning. The details are as follows:

This Year's Rainfall

According to the records of the Astronomical Observatory, from January to the end of May this year, there were a total of fifty-four days of rainfall in Shanghai, with a total rainfall of 13.37 inches. Compared with the rainfall of 10.27 inches in the same period last year, it exceeds the previous year by 3.1 feet. At the same time, the climate is far less favorable than the same period last year, which has greatly hindered agricultural production.

Cold Weather

Since the arrival of summer, the weather has remained persistently cold. Although there was a slight warming trend a few days ago, it suddenly changed the day before yesterday, with very strong winds all day. Wind and rain continued throughout the night, lasting until last night. The weather resembles late autumn, and warm clothing is needed. This kind of abnormal weather has rarely been seen in recent years.

Huangpu River Tide Recedes

Since the 4th of this month, the high tide in the Huangpu River has suddenly increased, with levels all above ten feet. The highest tide was at 1:54 AM on the 7th, when the water level was ten feet and four inches above the lowest tide. However, since yesterday, it has begun to recede.

Shanghai Local Court Detains Xu Wancheng; Xu Surrenders Himself, but the Judge Still Fears His Escape; Immediately Issued an Arrest Warrant and Sent Him to the Detention Center

Xu Wancheng, the editor of the Longwen Bookstore located at No. 3 Baiyang Alley, Zhonghua Road, west of the Dainanmen, published a special issue of the "Xu Wancheng Work Report" attached to the "Minbao" on the 3rd of this month. It contained an "Investigation into the Dark Side of China's Judiciary," and its content mostly targeted the Shanghai Local Court. It mentioned incidents such as the theft of handguns from the court's stolen goods warehouse and severely attacked the president of the court. The text also stated, "Shops that evade stamp duty should be punished. When executing these laws, it should target the main figures. This case should also be executed according to the law, and everyone should be treated equally." It also mentioned that court clerks often openly solicit money and finally claimed that Judge Zhao and others accepted bribes, among other accusations. It further stated that the judge reverses right and wrong and that it should be clearly stipulated that anyone doing so should be punished by death. The court could tolerate other attacks, but regarding the accusation of Zhao and others accepting bribes, Judges Zhao Yongzhou and Zhao Yuesheng requested that Xu Wancheng be summoned to testify and report the accusations. Xu claimed that he had copied it from another newspaper. Therefore, the prosecutor ordered him to present the newspaper as evidence on Monday. However, Xu not only had no such basis but also sent a letter to the "Minbao" legal column on the 5th, again claiming that the court was "covering up its face," etc. Therefore, the two Judges Zhao believed that if this case were not pursued, it would affect their careers. Therefore, they specifically filed a complaint as victims. Furthermore, Xu Wancheng had a debt case in Judge Zhao Yongzhou's hands and lost the case, which further indicated that he was seeking revenge. Judge Zhao did not pursue evidence of bribery. Therefore, the court continued its investigation yesterday. Xu sent a representative, Liu Lianyuan, to the court in the morning, but he was informed that criminal cases do not allow representatives, so it was not permitted. In the afternoon at 2:00 PM, Xu Wancheng personally surrendered himself. Prosecutor Tang Ruxiu immediately opened a court for preliminary interrogation. The judge asked him to produce the newspaper from which he claimed to have copied, but Xu could not respond and instead claimed that he was mentally disordered. The judge believed that Xu Wancheng's behavior was despicable and feared that he would escape once indicted. Therefore, the court ordered his detention and immediately issued an arrest warrant, sending Xu to the detention center.

Four Members of the Song Xihou Family in Sida Village, Remi Road, Attacked; Two Young Men in Western Suits Entered the House Under the Pretense of Delivering a Letter; Four People Were Shot, and Song Himself Died; The Patrol Believes There is Another Reason for This Case

Song Xihou, a Hua compradore who used to work for the British merchant Hezhelin Cotton Yarn Office, was from Yuyao, Zhejiang, and was 45 years old. His home was at No. 10, Sida Village, Dingjia Alley, No. 142 Remi Road, French Concession of Shanghai West. He retired three years ago. At 11:35 AM yesterday, Song was having lunch at home when two young men wearing Western suits suddenly came to talk to Song. After the servant reported, Song met them in the parlor on the second floor. Unexpectedly, before they had said a few words, the two young men took out handguns from their sleeves and attacked Song. One bullet hit Song's abdomen. At that time, Song's concubine, Cao (29 years old, from Changshu), and two Changshu maids, Du Chen (43 years old) and Yuan Xu (42 years old), heard the noise and rushed out. They happened to meet the two thugs. Fearing that things would go wrong, the two thugs fired several shots at the three, and all three fell to the ground after being hit. Cao was hit in the back of the head by a bullet that did not penetrate. Du Chen was hit weakly on the left cheek, and Yuan Xu was injured on the right leg. Fortunately, Song's daughter, Meizhen, heard the continuous gunshots upstairs and knew that something was wrong. Suspecting it was a robbery, she bravely ran to the balcony on the third floor and blew the police whistle frantically. Seeing that they had injured several people and hearing the police whistle, the two young men rushed out the door together and fled. Song's family members quickly called the patrol station. The patrol chief immediately sent Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. After a detailed investigation, they believed that this case was not a robbery and injury case, and that there might be another reason behind it. After the investigation, they first sent the four injured people to Guangci Hospital. Meanwhile, they started investigating the criminals. Song himself died after arriving at the hospital due to his serious injuries. His concubine, Cao, was also seriously injured and her life was in danger.

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Telegraphed Request to Waive Export Tax on Qingtian Stone

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing yesterday, stating: "To the Ministry of Finance, Nanjing. According to a letter from Zhou Huaixuan, a representative of the Qingtian Stone Carving Industry, dated the 6th of this month, Qingtian has many mountains and little land, and the land is barren and the people are poor. Women and children in the countryside rely on the Qingtian stone carving industry for their livelihood. Before the European War, exports to foreign countries could earn hundreds of thousands of yuan each year. Since then, tax rates have increased, and sales have gradually decreased. In recent years, income has been less than one hundred thousand yuan. Those who look to the roof and sigh, and cry in poverty, are struggling to maintain their livelihoods. Unexpectedly, the Ministry of Finance has increased the export tax on these carvings starting March 1st of this year. This will not only leave the common people with no hope for their livelihoods but will also affect the country's revenue. Exports of local products, such as paper umbrellas, straw mats, and embroidery from Wenzhou, are all tax-exempt. The essence of Qingtian stone is originally stubborn and difficult to split. After much hard work, carving can be accomplished. Labor is time-consuming, and the cost is no less than that of paper umbrellas. According to regulations, tax exemption should be requested to avoid regrets and to show fairness. Moreover, Qingtian has suffered from banditry, and most houses are empty. Farmers have lost their timing, and businesses are closed in the market. This handicraft industry, which is related to the poor, will also be cut off due to the increase in taxes. If no measures are taken, the good people will be forced to starve to death, and the unruly will take risks. Public security is also a concern. Therefore, we present this request, hoping that your association will consider the livelihoods of the poor in our county, provide assistance, and unanimously advocate for the exemption of this export tax to maintain industry and commerce. This would be a great blessing." We have investigated that when the country is facing rampant smuggling and a shortage of tax revenue, it is difficult to discuss reducing export tariffs. Even the association did not dare to request it rashly. However, it is claimed that the annual sales of Qingtian stone to foreign countries are less than one hundred thousand yuan. This export tax, even if calculated at 7.5% of the value, will still be less than one thousand yuan per year. If the tax is waived, it will not affect public funds, but it will greatly benefit the local handicraft industry. It is reasonable to report the situation to your department for review and approval. It would be a great convenience for the public. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce kowtows."

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Government to Request the Apprehension of Stolen Goods and Thieves from a Robbed Pig Boat

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Jiangsu Provincial Government in Zhenjiang yesterday, stating: "To the Jiangsu Provincial Government in Zhenjiang. According to a letter from the Fresh Pork Sales Industry Association dated the 15th of this month, we have received a letter from our colleagues Xi Jinyuan, Chen Xide, and others, stating that on the 8th of this month, they hired the Jin Yuanli sand boat from Rugao, their hometown, to transport 230 pigs to Shanghai for sale. Unexpectedly, at around 1:00 AM that night, when the boat passed the Eleventh Regiment Port, Tongzhou, on the opposite bank of Tiansheng Port, a pirate ship suddenly appeared. A dozen or so bandits, armed with six or seven long and short guns, speaking in mixed dialects, and making a lot of noise, ordered the boat to stop and plundered it at will. With a whoop, they rowed away fully loaded. After checking, 52 piglets were robbed, including 27 from Xi Jinyuan's Jincai brand and 25 from Chen Xide's Rencaiyuan brand, as well as 10 yuan in national currency, clothing, and other items, with a total loss of about 900 yuan. The pigs sold by Jinyuan and others are mostly obtained on credit. Once they suffer this disaster, their livelihood will be cut off. We are forced to report the facts and request that you forward them to the competent authorities for prompt arrest of the fugitive bandits, strict punishment according to the law, and recovery of the stolen goods. Then we will all be grateful." We have learned that robberies of pig boats occur from time to time. For example, on March 2nd of last year, Miao Changfa's boat was robbed of 46 piglets at the 200-mu area near Langshan outside the Wusong Estuary. On November 8th of the same year, Yang Baozhu's boat, transporting Tang Baoquan's piglets, was robbed of 52 piglets near Shiziling. Most recently, last month, Gu Zhengqing and Zhang Dalin's piglets were robbed of 35 piglets in the Baimao Sand area. In summary, the robbery locations are all on the main transportation routes between Shanghai and Jiangsu, where boats travel frequently and are prosperous. The bandits dare to gather and rob, which shows that the area is poorly guarded and endangers merchant ships. If they are allowed to remain at large, the consequences will be dire. Merchants may stop traveling and consider it a long journey. Based on the reported situation, we hereby request your association to promptly telegraph the competent official authorities of Jiangsu Province to order their subordinates to pursue and arrest the bandits and punish them severely so that the stolen goods can be returned to their original owners. This will not only benefit our industry but also rely on the local public security. We look forward to your assistance. We have checked that within the jurisdiction of Jiangsu Province, according to the association's information, there have been four pig boat robberies in the past year, and few have been solved. It is difficult to sleep peacefully for such freight transportation. The water public security team, which is responsible for patrolling and arresting, is responsible for the negligence. Based on the letter and the previous situation, it is appropriate to telegraph your government for review and approval, urging the water public security police team to tighten the investigation on the one hand, strive to recover the stolen goods and arrest the bandits, and patrol regularly on the other hand, so that the bandits will stop, and merchants will be safe. We look forward to it very much. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce kowtows."

Changyin Chinese Knitting Factory Trademark Printed Illegally; Local Court Summoned Yesterday

Cai Yinqiao, the owner of the Shanghai China First Knitting Factory on Sichuan Road, found out that Changyin, a printing house located at Jincheng Printing House, Anlan Road, West Gate, was illegally printing the trademark of his factory. He reported it to the police, who searched and seized seven counterfeit printing molds. The shop owner, Jin Zubei, and his partner, Yang Boliang, were arrested, and more than 100,000 trademark papers were copied. After questioning, it was learned that the above-mentioned trademark paper was entrusted by Yang Ruijin, the owner of Hengda Printing House at No. 99, Siwenli, Xinzha Road. Yang was arrested and confessed that he was instructed by Fa Xian to print. Li was also arrested, and hundreds of fake trademarks were copied, mixed with four pairs of black chrysanthemum brand inferior socks, and sent to the local court. In addition to the defendants being temporarily released on bail, the prosecutor is now prosecuting the defendants together. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu opened the trial. Cai Yinqiao testified, "I am fifty-seven years old. I received letters from the outside world in the second half of last year saying that someone was selling Changyin brand socks. I started investigating and only found out on May 2nd that Jincheng Printing House was at No. 8, Ningkangli, Four Gates. The second defendant is Jin Zubei, and Yang Boliang is his partner. A total of seven fresh flower zinc plates and trademarks were seized, and Yang Ruijin was the co-conspirator." Defendant Yang Boliang testified, "I am twenty-two years old, from Shaoxing. I am a partner at Jin Zubei's place. On May 2nd, I was arrested by the police at 11:30 PM. Seven fresh flower zinc plates were copied, which were entrusted by others to print. A total of 105,000 copies were printed, with a price of 34 yuan, etc." Jin Zubei testified, "I am forty-six years old, from Shaoxing. I run the Jincheng Printing House. The black chrysanthemum trademark was printed on behalf of Yang Ruijin. Yang also runs a printing house, but he cannot print it himself, so he entrusted me to print it," and so on. At this point, the judge said, "Li Zaixian and Yang Ruijin have not arrived today. They should be summoned again for questioning."
